# Ralph Pipeline — Roadmap

**Last updated:** March 23, 2026 (Session: CT9 transition-slot visibility ban + C1 timeout fix + RULE-003 transitionScreen try/catch (dc03155, 4e8fca8, 2026-03-23); PART-028 stripped-CSS T1 check + FIX-001 preserve-CSS rule + ARIA-001 feedback accessibility (dc03155); Slack parent message live updates at step boundaries (9101650); Cross-slot feed links — UI/UX findings route to R&D + test quality + education (4f96009); Cron 7 Slot Watchdog — idle slot detection every 5 min (c57447d); per-game docs consolidated into warehouse/templates/ (7935d5d); R&D slot ACTIVE: post-GEN-116/117/118 first-attempt approval rate measurement (2/5 data points); Education slot ACTIVE: which-ratio #560 re-queued after EACCES infra fix; UI/UX slot: face-memory #512 browser audit DONE — 0 P0 + 6 findings (3 MEDIUM systemic, 3 LOW); next target: expression-completer #511)

## P8 — Build Reliability (from failure-analysis.md, 2026-03-20)

> Source: `docs/failure-analysis.md` — 223 builds analyzed. Warehouse gate + BullMQ stall fix address 63% of production failures.

| Item | Status | Files | Notes |
|------|--------|-------|-------|
| **Warehouse hygiene gate** | **done (2026-03-20)** | worker.js, lib/pipeline.js | Pre-build: deletes stale warehouse HTML for non-approved games before calling `runPipeline()`. Prevents generation bypass — root cause of 54% of production failures. Shipped in commit 8202a79. |
| **BullMQ stall prevention** | **done (2026-03-20)** | worker.js | Wired `onProgress` → `job.updateProgress()` every ~2 min (KillMode=control-group + heartbeat). BullMQ renews job lock on each call, preventing the 15 stall failures. Shipped in commit cc36e6c. |
| **Stale warehouse auto-delete: relax isInitFailure guard** | **done (2026-03-20)** | lib/pipeline.js | `isInitFailure()` refactored to exported function; ANY-match + passed===0; 14 regex patterns; 10 new unit tests; 399 tests pass; deployed 2026-03-20 (commit 5e7eaa0). |
| **Redis AOF persistence (Task #44)** | **done (2026-03-20)** | docker-compose.yml | `--appendonly yes` in Redis service command prevents BullMQ queue loss on restart. Verified on live server: `ralph-redis-1` container running with AOF active; `appendonlydir/` with `*.incr.aof` confirmed. See Lesson 45 in docs/lessons-learned.md. |
| **Step 1d: Page load smoke check** | **done (2026-03-20)** | lib/pipeline-utils.js, lib/pipeline.js | `runPageSmokeDiagnostic()` + `classifySmokeErrors()` added. Catches CDN 404s, `waitForPackages` timeout, init errors before test-gen runs. One regen attempt on fatal errors; throws immediately if still broken. 11 new tests; 428 total pass. See Lesson 46 in docs/lessons-learned.md. |
| **Global fix 0/0 regression: page broken after global fix** | **done (2026-03-21, commit 25ca9e6)** | lib/pipeline-fix-loop.js | Pattern observed in count-and-tap #393, #397 and word-pairs #395 global fix loop. Fix: (1) track pre-global-fix HTML and which batches were passing before each iteration; (2) detect when a previously-passing batch regresses to 0/0 after global fix; (3) roll back to pre-fix HTML and log a warning; (4) capture browser console errors via `capturePageConsoleErrors()` and inject as `brokenPageErrorContext` into next global fix prompt. 550 tests pass. Measure: count-and-tap #440 is the first build that will exercise this guard. |
| **BullMQ lock duration 90min → 5h + stalledInterval 30s → 5min** | **done (2026-03-21, commit 17b384d)** | worker.js | Root cause: `updateProgress()` does NOT renew BullMQ lock (incorrect prior comments); lock renewal is solely by LockManager timer. 90min lockDuration was insufficient for 5-iteration builds (5×25-30min = 125-150min total). stalledInterval=30s caused premature stall detection on any transient Redis blip → double-execution race ("Missing key for job N. moveToFinished"). Fix: lockDuration 90min→5h, lockRenewTime 20min→60min, stalledInterval default→5min. 550 tests pass. Prevents double-execution and premature stall detection on long builds. |

| **TE-ANALYTICS-001: adjustment-strategy toBeVisible() failures** | **DIAGNOSED — 2026-03-23** | **Verdict: TEST BUG (historical, now resolved — game approved on build #385).** Root causes were two distinct test-gen bugs: (1) Early builds (#376–#378, failure_patterns IDs 3–14): test-gen generated `toBeVisible()` assertions on game-play elements WITHOUT first calling `startGame()` — violated R1/phase-gated visibility. (2) Build #381: `#mathai-transition-slot button` used as locator in mechanics/level-progression/edge-cases/contract tests — all timed out because slot is empty after startGame() — violated GF9/R2. Build #378 HTML was structurally correct (CDN packages loaded, `transitionScreen.show()` called, `data-phase=start_screen` synced properly). This is a pure test-gen bug, not an HTML bug. **Cross-game pattern confirmed:** Same `#mathai-transition-slot button` not-toBeVisible() failure is ACTIVE in recent failed builds: find-triangle-side #547, name-the-sides #553–556, keep-track #483, associations #513-pre — all contract.spec.js. The fix rules GF5/GF9/R2/R2/CT3 already exist in prompts.js; failure pattern persists because generated contract tests still use direct `#mathai-transition-slot button` selector instead of `skipToEnd()`. **Proposed fix:** Add a T1-style pre-test-gen check or strengthen GF9/CT3 with a BANNED-SELECTOR list. | **timer.start() must only appear in renderRound() — never in setupGame()** | **pending** | setupGame() calling timer.start() then renderRound() calling timer.reset() creates a race: if timer fires onEnd before renderRound() reaches it, handleTimeout() runs with currentQuestion===null. Fix: remove timer.start() from setupGame(); only call timer.start() inside renderRound(). Add to CDN_CONSTRAINTS_BLOCK TIMER LIFECYCLE rule. Source: addition-mcq-blitz spec audit. | Eliminates handleTimeout(null) crash on slow devices at game start. |
| **All signalCollector calls must precede seal() — never call recordViewEvent after seal()** | **pending** | showResults() calling signalCollector.recordViewEvent() AFTER signalCollector.seal() in endGame() records into a finalised payload and silently loses the event. Fix: add to CDN_CONSTRAINTS_BLOCK: "seal() must be the last SignalCollector call in endGame(); move any recordViewEvent calls to before seal()." Source: addition-mcq-blitz spec audit. | Prevents silent analytics data loss at results screen in every game. |
| **endGame() for lives games must explicitly branch game-over vs victory TransitionScreen** | **pending** | Lives games need two different TransitionScreen.show() calls: game-over path (lives=0) with stars=0 and "Try again!" button vs victory path (lives>0) with stars=1-3 and "Play again!" button. | **TEST gap: window.nextRound alias missing for loadRound()-based games** | **pending** | lib/prompts.js (test-gen) | Source: UI/UX audit adjustment-strategy #385 (F6). Harness warns MISSING window.nextRound at load. Game uses `loadRound()` which is exposed as `window.loadRound` — harness `jumpToRound()` falls back to `window.loadRound()`, so functional impact may be low. | **GEN rule: never negate a guard flag immediately after checking it** | **pending** | lib/prompts.js | Source: UI/UX audit count-and-tap #551 (UI-CT-004). Pattern: `if (!isActive) return; isActive = false; isActive = true;` — guard is defeated the instant it fires. Pattern left behind by fix-loop LLMs that add temporary lock flags then immediately undo them. Fix: gen prompt rule: "Never assign a flag to false and then immediately to true — this defeats the guard and is dead code. If the guard is not needed, remove it. Use `answerLocked` or `isProcessing` as the single source of truth for double-click protection." |
| **GEN rule: progressBar.update() arg must be clamped to valid range** | **pending** | lib/prompts.js | Source: UI/UX audit name-the-sides (UI-NS-007). `progressBar.update(-9)` fires PAGEERROR every round — negative count value is invalid. Fix: gen prompt rule requiring progressBar.update() argument to be clamped to [0, totalRounds] before call. Also: T1 check for progressBar.update() calls with literal negative constants. Measure: zero progressBar PAGEERROR in next 3 CDN builds using ProgressBarComponent. |
| **Re-run T1 validation on targeted fix HTML before Playwright** | **DONE (0f84035, 2026-03-23)** | lib/pipeline-targeted-fix.js, lib/prompts.js, lib/pipeline-fix-loop.js | Root cause: targeted fix LLM generates patched HTML → T1 errors not injected into retry prompt → CSS-stripped HTML passes Playwright (DOM state asserted, not rendering) → approved game visually broken. Fix shipped: (1) T1 errors captured after each fix attempt; (2) injected as context into next retry via `t1ErrorContext` param in `buildTargetedFixPrompt`; (3) graceful degradation after 2 consecutive T1 failures — proceed to Playwright rather than blocking pipeline; (4) `runStaticValidationLocal` exported + 5 unit tests added. Would have caught CSS stripping in name-the-sides #557 and which-ratio #560. 1065 tests pass. |
| **Local verification workflow: download-apply-test before build queue** | **pending** | docs/areas/local-verification.md | When a gen rule or T1 check is shipped, current workflow is: deploy → queue build → wait 30 min → discover if fix works. New workflow: deploy → download most recent relevant failed HTML from GCP → apply fix to HTML → run Playwright locally → if passes, queue build. Creates docs/areas/local-verification.md documenting the standard local verification process (curl GCP HTML, inject fix, run diagnostic.js, run Playwright). Reduces fix verification from 30 min to 5-10 min. |
| **TEST gap: TC-005 timeout test (46s wait) will cause slow test suite** | **pending** | lib/prompts.js test-gen | Source: stats-median UI/UX audit (2026-03-23). TC-005 spec requires waiting 46 seconds for timer expiry — this is correct behaviour but will be generated as a real 46s `page.waitForTimeout(46000)` in the edge-cases test. For timer games, test-gen should call `window.gameState.timer.pause()` + directly invoke `handleTimeout()` via `window.handleTimeout()` instead of waiting the full timer duration. Reduces edge-case test time from 46s → <1s. Needs window.handleTimeout exposed in spec (similar to window.loadQuestion). | Low |

### Cross-game learning injection — design notes

- **Source**: `learnings` table already populated per build (`level`, `category`, `content`). APPROVED builds are ground truth.
- **Retrieval**: at Step 1 (gen) and Step 3 (fix), query `learnings WHERE resolved=0` for games sharing the same PART set (parsed from spec CDN section). Top-N by recency + category relevance.
- **Injection**: append as `## Lessons from similar games` block to gen/fix system prompt — same slot as spec-derived hints.
- **Scope**: `pipeline.js` only. No new DB schema (learnings table already exists). No new env var needed.
- **Success metric**: average iterations-to-pass drops; track via `builds.iterations` across next 10 builds post-deploy.

| 2026-03-23 | lib/validate-static.js + test/validate-static.test.js | **CR-091 [PASS / 2 WARNs] — GEN-112 paren-depth fix edge case review (commit 8f1e41a).** Reviewed paren-depth-aware `progressBar.update()` 3-arg detector (lines 690–710). Tested 6 edge cases. **PASS — Case A** `progressBar.update(gameState.currentRound, Math.max(0, gameState.lives))`: 0 top-level commas after depth-tracking; correctly NOT flagged. **PASS — Case B** `progressBar.update(round, lives, extra)`: 2 top-level commas; correctly flagged. **PASS — Case C** `progressBar.update(round, fn(a, b, c))`: nested commas at depth>0; 1 top-level comma; correctly NOT flagged. **PASS — Case D** multiline 2-arg: `[^;]*?` lazy quantifier matches across newlines (`[^;]` is NOT dot — newlines are NOT semicolons, so multiline calls are matched and depth-counted correctly). **WARN-1 [FALSE POSITIVE — LOW RISK] — Case E: string literals and comments.** The regex matches `progressBar.update(a, b, c)` inside comment lines (`// progressBar.update(a, b, c)`) and string literals (`console.log('progressBar.update(a, b, c)')`). Cannot distinguish code from comment/string context without a full JS parser. Risk: LOW — LLM-generated games never include commented-out 3-arg update calls; the pattern only appears in actual code. No fix needed. **PASS — Case F:** Two calls on same line correctly isolated by the lazy `[^;]*?` (terminates at `)` not at `;`); both calls captured independently by `/g` flag; only the 3-arg call is flagged. **WARN-2 [FALSE NEGATIVE — THEORETICAL] — `[^;]*?` truncation on inline semicolons.** If a multiline `progressBar.update()` arg contains a semicolon (e.g. a comment `// note; see above` on the same logical line, or a statement-style expression), `[^;]*?` terminates early and the `)` is never reached — the entire call is silently dropped from `updateMatches`. Verified: `progressBar.update(\n  round,\n  getVal(); // comment\n  lives\n)` → truncated match, 3-arg call missed. Risk: THEORETICAL ONLY — no valid JS expression argument contains a bare semicolon. Fixing would require replacing `[^;]*?` with a depth-aware full match (significant complexity); not warranted. **Tests:** 249/249 pass. Existing tests (lines 1047–1085) cover Cases A and B. Cases C–F not independently tested; low value given risk assessments above. | — |
| 2026-03-23 | lib/pipeline-fix-loop.js + lib/pipeline.js | **CR-090 [PASS — already fixed] — fixCdnDomainsInFile/fixCdnPathsInFile call coverage in fix-loop LLM write paths.** CR-070 identified two LLM HTML write paths in pipeline-fix-loop.js lacking CDN domain/path normalization: (1) warehouse-regen path (line 897) and (2) per-iteration fix write (line 1443). Both paths now call `if (ctx.fixCdnDomainsInFile) await ctx.fixCdnDomainsInFile(htmlFile)` + `ctx.fixCdnPathsInFile(htmlFile)` before `injectHarnessToFile()` (lines 898–899 and 1459–1460). `ctx` is constructed in pipeline.js lines 1232–1233 with both functions passed directly. Both functions are synchronous — `await` on them resolves immediately, no concern. Minor note: calls omit the optional `logger` arg so CDN-fix warnings route to `console.warn` instead of the structured pipeline logger. Low severity — no action needed (both functions have `logger` as optional with `console.warn` default). No code change required. | — |
| 2026-03-23 | lib/validate-static.js | **CR-092 [HIGH RISK — FIXED (1741e83)] — GEN-DOM-CACHE `[^{}]*` false negative: nested blocks before getElementById silently missed.** `[^{}]*` stops at the first closing brace — any per-round function with an `if`/`for`/`try` block before `getElementById` passes the check silently. Risk: HIGH — real generated functions almost always have nested blocks. Fix: imperative brace-depth scanner (extractFunctionBody helper) — walks forward tracking depth, extracts complete function body, then tests for DOM calls. Option B (one-level unrolling) rejected as fragile. Option A (depth scanner) implemented by sub-agent. ~30 lines. +2 regression tests for `if`-nested and `for`-nested cases. | Gen Quality (brace-depth scanner — in flight) |
| 2026-03-23 | lib/validate-static.js | **CR-086 [FIXED] — GEN-ROUND-INDEX false positive on `loadRound =` pattern.** `loadRound\s*=[\s\S]{0,200}nextRound\s*\(` uses `[\s\S]` which crosses closing braces — fires on correct code where `window.loadRound = function(n){...};` is followed by an unrelated `nextRound()` call in a subsequent `addEventListener`. Fixed to `[^}]{0,200}` so the window cannot cross a `}`. Also documents: (a) GEN-PM-DUAL-PATH false negative — nested if/try-catch inside the victory block before `postMessage` breaks the `[^}]*` match; (b) GEN-PM-DUAL-PATH does NOT catch `if (gameState.gameWon)` style guards (only string `'victory'`); (c) GEN-TESTID-RESTART misses `retry-btn`, `button-restart`, `restartButton` variants. 9 unit tests added (3 per rule: bug fires → passes, multiline/variant bug fires → passes, correct HTML → no warn). 1184/1184 tests pass. Commit: fix(code-review): CR-086. | — |
| 2026-03-23 | lib/categorize-failure.js | **CR-058 [FIXED] — categorizeFailure() missed multi-line Playwright numeric diff format.** The existing branch `/expected:\s*\d.*received:\s*\d/i` requires both values on one line. Playwright emits them on separate lines: `Expected: 2\nReceived: 1`. These fell through to `'unknown'`. Fix: added second branch `/expected:\s*[\d"'][\s\S]*?received:\s*[\d"']/i` using `[\s\S]*?` to span newlines. 2 unit tests added (branch 15b). Commit eea041e. | 2026-03-23 | lib/prompts.js | **CR-072 [WARN] — GEN-TESTID-STEP (rule 57) + GEN-WINDOW-NEXTROUNDEXPOSED (rule 58) absent from buildGenerationPrompt numbered list:** Both rules are present in CDN_CONSTRAINTS_BLOCK (lines 313–314, inline one-liner form) and in buildCliGenPrompt (lines 1510, 1514 inline form). Every other rule from GEN-RESTART-RESET, GEN-PHASE-ALL, GEN-TRANSITION-ICONS, GEN-MCQ-PHASE etc. appears in all three locations as a numbered entry. Rules 57 and 58 land in only 2/3 locations. | 2026-03-23 | lib/prompts.js | **CR-073 [WARN] — GEN-TESTID-STEP scope ambiguity (sequential-visibility vs. concurrent-DOM):** The rule triggers on "multiple sequential interactive steps that coexist in the DOM simultaneously" but the WRONG/RIGHT example shows step panels that are hidden/shown (display:none toggle), not truly concurrent. GEN-STEP-001 already mandates hiding all non-active panels. If a game follows GEN-STEP-001 correctly, only step1-panel is ever visible — yet GEN-TESTID-STEP still applies because ALL panels exist in the DOM at once (just with display:none). The current wording "coexist in the DOM simultaneously" is correct but could be read as "simultaneously visible". LLM may hesitate to apply the rule when panels are hidden. Fix needed: replace "coexist in the DOM simultaneously" with "exist in the DOM at the same time (regardless of display:none or visibility:hidden state) — querySelector always hits the first DOM match even when panels are hidden". | Gen Quality backlog |
| 2026-03-23 | lib/prompts.js | **CR-074 [WARN] — GEN-WINDOW-NEXTROUNDEXPOSED no-op risk: rule says "single-round game OR no concept of next round → define window.nextRound = () => {}" — but provides no definition of "single-round". The LLM could interpret any non-advancing game (e.g. a worked-example with multiple question panels but no explicit "round" loop) as single-round and add a useless no-op, hiding a genuine missing-nextRound bug. LOW risk since adding a no-op is safe (harness calls it, nothing happens), but can mask real omissions. Recommendation: add a clarifying note: "If in doubt, expose the real advance function; only use no-op when the spec explicitly says the game ends after a single interaction sequence". | Gen Quality low-backlog |

| 2026-03-23 | lib/mcp.js | **CR-080 [WARN] — register_spec write path lacks path.resolve() confinement check.** gameId regex `/^[a-zA-Z0-9-]+$/` (line 304) blocks all traversal vectors (dots, slashes, backslashes, percent-encoded chars) — not currently exploitable. However, the write path (`path.join(REPO, 'warehouse', 'templates', game_id, 'spec.md')`) has no `path.resolve()` + `startsWith()` guard, unlike `readWarehouseFile()` which correctly applies that check (lines 40–42). Asymmetric hardening: reads are guarded, writes are not. If regex is ever relaxed or a new input path is introduced, the write side has no backstop. Recommendation: add `path.resolve()` confinement check on templateDir before mkdirSync, matching readWarehouseFile pattern. | Code — low severity, defense-in-depth |

Minor gap; acceptable. **COMMIT a3f0a4a — OVERALL: PASS WITH FINDINGS.** Regex `/totalLives\s*:\s*(?:0+\b|-\d)/` correctly catches `0`, `00`, `-1`, `-5`. Does not fire on `1`, `3`, `10`. **CR-032 [MED] — Regex fires false positive on `totalLives: 0.5`:** `\b` is a word boundary between a word character (`0`) and a non-word character (`.`) — so `0+\b` fires before the `.` in `0.5`. A float totalLives is also a bug so this is arguably a true positive, but the error message says "0 or negative" — a `0.5` message would be confusing. Practical risk low (no confirmed instance of float totalLives). **CR-033 [LOW] — `-\d` only matches one digit but partial-match semantics mean -10, -100 ARE caught:** The task analysis flagged `-\d` as only catching one digit. In practice, `/(?:0+\b|-\d)/` is applied via `.test()` which performs a partial match — `-\d` matches the first two chars `-1` of `-10`, so the test fires for `-10`, `-100`, `-999`. This is the correct behavior (all negatives should fire). The commit message was slightly misleading but the behavior is correct. Word boundary `\b` in `0+\b`: confirmed that `totalLives: 0.5` fires (dot is non-word, see CR-032). `totalLives: 05` does NOT fire (`0+\b` requires word boundary after the zero sequence, but `5` is a word character — no boundary). Since `05 === 5` in JS strict mode (not octal), this is a true negative (5 lives is valid). Unit tests cover: `0`, `-1`, `-5`, `00` (fail); `1`, `3` (pass). Edge cases not tested: `-10` (passes but for partial-match reason), `0.5` (fires — false positive, see CR-032), `0px` (does not fire — correct). | Gen Quality (CR-030 HIGH — verify signalCollector.reset() CDN API or switch to safe re-instantiation), Gen Quality (CR-031 LOW — duplicate CR-025), Gen Quality (CR-032 MED — false positive on 0.5) |

| 2026-03-23 | lib/prompts.js (buildTestGenCategoryPrompt GF1 block, extractPhaseNamesFromGame, ~L992–1029) | **P2 — extractUserScenarios `descMatch` regex is too greedy on long specs (prompts.js ~L900):** Pattern `/Description[:\s]+(.+?)(?:\n\n|\n##|\n\|)/is` uses lazy `.+?` with the `s` flag (dotAll) — the `s` flag makes `.` match newlines, so `.+?` can span multiple lines. The lazy quantifier stops at the first `\n\n`, `\n##`, or `\n|`. But if the Description section has no blank line before the next section (a spec formatting quirk), the regex may consume the entire spec body and the `desc` string becomes the rest of the file. The subsequent `if (/adjust|…/i.test(desc))` checks on a multi-thousand-character `desc` are harmless (false positives are bounded — only up to 4 extra scenarios), and deduplication + `slice(0,7)` cap prevents overflow. Actual impact: at most 1–2 spurious scenarios injected into the test-gen prompt. **Route:** Gen Quality — low priority; constrain regex to `[^#]{0,400}` or remove `s` flag. | Gen Quality |

DOM snapshot now contains real `.choice-btn` and `.option-btn` elements — no longer misleading. **GF9-ENFORCEMENT PASS:** 6 trigger phrases listed are representative of the real LLM failure patterns ("start screen to game start", "game starts when start is clicked", "transition to playing", "screen advances to game", "start button starts game", "clicking start shows game screen"). Root-cause attribution (19/70 GF failures) is credible and correctly cited. Placement immediately after GF9 is correct — high LLM attention position. Instruction to use `startGame(page)` + `waitForPhase('playing', 15000)` is the correct fix. **CR-017 [LOW] — GF9-ENFORCEMENT trigger phrases use substring matching but the rule says "contains these phrases":** LLM test names commonly include variants like "verifies transition from start to playing", "tests that game starts on click", or "clicking the start button transitions state" that do not match any listed phrase literally. The enforcement block is a prompt instruction, not a runtime regex, so partial coverage is expected — but the listed set covers the most common prefix-exact forms only. No immediate fix needed; worth expanding if a new false-negative is observed in logs. **GF10 PASS:** Rule correctly gates on step panel presence (step1-panel, step2-panel, example-panel, faded-panel, practice-panel) and explains WHY `answer(page, true)` fails (generic helper only matches .answer-btn/.option-btn/.choice-btn). WRONG/RIGHT examples are concrete and correct. Root cause citations (real-world-problem #564, find-triangle-side #549, quadratic-formula #545/#546) add LLM credibility. No edge cases missed for the current known step-panel game set. **CR-002 .answer-btn M16 PASS:** Third M16 pattern added correctly. `getComputedStyle(el).minHeight` with `parseInt()` is the right approach for checking CSS property (not rendered height) — consistent with GEN-UX-002 intent. Two new tests cover: (1) DOM snapshot trigger when `.answer-btn` present, (2) `getComputedStyle`/`minHeight` present in assertion — both correctly structured. **CR-018 [MED] — .answer-btn uses getComputedStyle(minHeight) but .choice-btn/.option-btn use getBoundingClientRect().height — inconsistent measurement methods:** `.choice-btn` and `.option-btn` patterns use `el.getBoundingClientRect().height` (rendered height), while `.answer-btn` uses `parseInt(getComputedStyle(el).minHeight)` (CSS property). If CSS `min-height:44px` is set but padding makes rendered height >44px, both methods pass. But if `min-height` is not set and the element reaches 44px via padding alone, `getComputedStyle(el).minHeight` returns `'0px'` (no min-height declaration) and `parseInt('0px')===0 < 44` — the test FAILS even though the button is visually 44px tall. The GEN-UX-002 spec intent is to enforce the CSS property itself (not just rendered height), so the `getComputedStyle` approach is arguably correct. But the inconsistency creates a higher false-fail rate for `.answer-btn` games that use padding-based sizing. **Route:** Gen Quality — decide policy: either standardize all three to `getBoundingClientRect().height` (rendered, permissive) or all three to `getComputedStyle(el).minHeight` (CSS property, strict). Document the decision in M16. **GEN-112 wrong-args expansion PASS:** The new single-line GEN-112 at line 833 (in buildCliGenPrompt) is technically correct — it adds the `progressBar.update()` wrong-args anti-patterns (totalRounds as 2nd arg) that the original GEN-112 at line 768 did NOT cover. Root cause attribution (which-ratio #559/#560/#561, "RangeError: Invalid count value: -5") is accurate and high-credibility. **CR-019 [MED] — DONE (d76ecb0, 2026-03-23)** — GEN-112 wrong-args block added to buildGenerationPrompt() as rule 38, matching CLI version. API-path games now receive CRITICAL WRONG PATTERNS warning for progressBar.update(gameState.currentRound, gameState.totalRounds). 988/988 tests pass. Deployed. | Gen Quality (CR-018 open), Test Engineering (CR-017 backlog) |
| 2026-03-23 | lib/pipeline-test-gen.js (887e76d: checkResultsScreenViewport rectTop guard; 7d7c2be: checkTransitionScreenContent; b66270a: M18 GEN-DATA-LIVES-GUARD; 34d7fa8: LP-2 banned-selector substitution) | **CR-049 MED**: checkResultsScreenViewport relies on caller calling waitForPhase first — no internal waitForSelector; skipped guard silently passes when element zero-size (timing gap). **CR-050 LOW**: checkTransitionScreenContent race — CDN auto-dismiss before page.evaluate() runs returns found:false, silent skip, bug goes undetected. **CR-051 LOW**: M18+M17 overlap — two conflicting guard styles (return vs test.skip) for same scenario; LLM may apply M17 and skip M18 test.skip variant; NO_LIVES_ASSERT lint rule is backstop. **CR-052 MED**: LP-2 substitution misses `.first().click()` form — regex at line 571 has no optional `.first()` group unlike line 576 which covers `.first().toBeVisible()`; banned selector passes through to emitted spec unchanged. **CR-053 LOW**: testCases JSON parse errors silently swallowed at lines 99/107; corrupt test-cases.json produces empty testCases → 0-test build with no error. **CR-054 LOW**: lintGeneratedTests runs all rules line-by-line even multiline patterns (no match, not a bug). | CR-052 → Test Engineering (banned selector escapes post-processing); CR-049 → Gen Quality (add waitForPhase call guard); CR-053 → pipeline-test-gen fixup |
| 2026-03-23 | worker.js (c688f0e: CODE-001 resolveFailurePattern on approval path; full file review) | **CR-055 MED**: `handleFixJob()` APPROVED path never calls `resolveFailurePattern()` — CODE-001 fix (c688f0e) only patched the main build path. A targeted fix job that gets APPROVED leaves all prior failure patterns permanently unresolved. Fix: add `getFailurePatterns(gameId).filter(!resolved)` + `resolveFailurePattern()` loop in `handleFixJob` after the `report.status === 'APPROVED'` check (~line 286). **CR-056 MED**: Final GCP upload (~lines 1165–1176) uses bare `await gcp.uploadGameArtifact(...)` with no `.catch()`. If the upload throws (e.g. GCP credential expiry), the exception reaches the top-level crash guard, which calls `db.failBuild()` and overwrites the already-written `db.completeBuild()` record — an APPROVED build flips to FAILED in DB after a working pipeline run. Fix: wrap in `try { ... } catch (gcpErr) { logger.warn(...) }` as done for all cosmetic uploads. **CR-057 LOW**: `extractLearnings()` has no dedup guard — calls `db.addLearning()` unconditionally. AUTO_RETRY or manual re-queues produce duplicate learning rows for the same game+failure content. Fix: check for existing `(gameId, content)` pair before inserting. **CR-058 LOW**: `categorizeFailure()` does not match the two-line Playwright numeric diff format (`Expected: 2\nReceived: 1`) — the `expected:\s*\d.*received:\s*\d` regex requires both on one line; multi-line output falls through to `'unknown'`. Fix: add multiline flag or a separate `/expected:[\s\S]*?received:/i` branch. **CR-059 LOW**: In the auto-retry block (~line 1216), `buildQueue` is only closed on the happy path after `buildQueue.add()`. If the skip-branch (`retry_count >= 1`) or null-Queue branch is hit, `buildQueue` is never closed — dangling Redis connection per retry-skip event. Fix: wrap in try/finally with `await buildQueue?.close()`. | CR-055 → worker.js fix (handleFixJob resolve patterns); CR-056 → worker.js fix (GCP upload error isolation — HIGH priority); CR-057 → backlog (analytics dedup); CR-058 → categorize-failure.js; CR-059 → worker.js fix (Queue close leak) |

40. **[SHIPPED] Sentry.Integrations.CaptureConsole fix** — commit 14b15d1; initSentry() template updated to remove deprecated `new Sentry.Integrations.CaptureConsole(...)` usage; T1 static check added. Eliminates face-memory and similar CDN game Step 1d failures. P6 item marked done.
52. **[SHIPPED] BullMQ "Missing key" lock expiry fix (R&D #52)** — commit 4af2fd2; root cause: two successive SIGKILL cycles (systemctl restart while builds running) corrupted BullMQ stall-set `stc` field, causing `moveToFinished` to find job hash missing after 49-min pipeline completion. Fix: (1) `maxStalledCount: 0` — prevents stall checker from ever accumulating `stc` field regardless of restart cycles; (2) "Missing key" error now logged as WARN not ERROR, skipped for Sentry — pure BullMQ bookkeeping noise after SIGKILL; (3) SIGTERM handler logs active build IDs explicitly so restarts are visibly warned. Deploy pending (worker.js staged at /tmp/worker.js — deploy after current builds 473+475 complete).
41. **[SHIPPED] Smoke-regen #gameContent recovery improvement (R&D #41)** — commit e0e302a; buildSmokeRegenFixPrompt() now includes CRITICAL CDN GAME INIT FIXES section: explicit WRONG vs CORRECT ScreenLayout.inject() showing missing `slots:` wrapper, full CDN `<script src>` tag template with exact URLs for helpers/components/feedback-manager, and initSentry() ordering rule (must be AFTER waitForPackages resolves). Previous prompt described the symptom but did not show the LLM how to identify the bug in the failing HTML. Targets 38.5% repeat-failure baseline. Next data points from visual-memory #476 and keep-track #477 will measure impact. Success criterion: repeat-failure rate drops below 20% over next 10 smoke-regen events.

Supersedes cc8eb56 + 4e0bf96 which went wrong direction.
